## 1: Prompt 1

Optimize the substrate kernel in /workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p29/optimization_rounds/round2/output_model_new.py

Use MFMA instructions `S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32` to do matrix multiplications and loads the data from global memory using vectorized loads S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4. The MFMA instruction computes 32x32x8 matmul cooperatively in a wave. Build larger tiles by issuing multiple MFMA instructions across K and output subtiles.
  
MFMA swizzle invariants:
  For A, `i in [0,32)`, `j in [0,8)`: `A(i, j) -> (lane_id = i + (j / 4) * 32, element = j % 4)`
  For B, `j in [0,8)`, `i in [0,32)`: `B(j, i) -> (lane_id = j + (i / 4) * 32, element = i % 4)`

Accumulator invariant for C: for each lane in [0, 64) and acc_idx in [0, 16):
  - col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
  - row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)

Do not invent a different unpacking. Do not use a naive acc_idx -> contiguous row mapping. Treat this mapping as fixed when writing results.

Stage A and B through LDS. Each thread loads operand fragments in 16-byte chunks. Treat each 16-byte fragment as `(4, S.u32)` and reinterpret it as `2 x (4, S.bf16)`. Feed both `(4, S.bf16)` halves into MFMA in natural order. The intended effect is a cooperative `32x32x16` accumulation from two natural MFMA steps. Do not add lane-dependent or K-dependent control flow to select halves.
  - The two `(4, S.bf16)` halves from one 16-byte LDS load collectively represent a swizzled `32x16` operand contribution with 4-column interleaving.
  - Consuming them in natural order must produce the same final C as a naive conceptual layout because operand pairings remain consistent under MFMA swizzle.

Scale the kernel from one wave to four waves without changing the MFMA per-wave invariant. Interpret the 4 warps as a 2 x 2 warp grid. Keep MFMA math identical per warp. Only add warp ownership offsets at operand fetch and output writeback.

Note:

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import substrate
import substrate.language as S

SQRT_2 = 1.4142135623730951

BATCH_SIZE = 1024
IN_FEATURES = 8192
OUT_FEATURES = 8192
BLOCK_M = 64
BLOCK_N = 64
WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
WAVE_SIZE = 64
BLOCK_THREADS = WAVES_PER_BLOCK * WAVE_SIZE
K_TILE = 16


def _launch():
    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))


@substrate.jit
def fused_kernel(
    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
    W: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
    BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
    x_range_bytes: S.i32,
    w_range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
    warp_row = warp // 2
    warp_col = warp % 2

    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    elem_bytes = S.convert(2, S.i32)
    x_stride = S.convert(IN_FEATURES, S.i32)
    w_stride = S.convert(IN_FEATURES, S.i32)

    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, x_range_bytes)
    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, w_range_bytes)

    shared_a = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
    shared_b = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)

    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    for k_base in S.range(0, IN_FEATURES, K_TILE):
        a_row = block_row + (warp_row * 32) + (lane % 32)
        a_k = k_base + (lane // 32) * 8
        a_offset = S.convert((a_row * x_stride + a_k) * elem_bytes, S.i32)
        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)

        if lane < 32:
            shared_a[warp_row, lane, 0] = a_packed[0]
            shared_a[warp_row, lane, 1] = a_packed[1]
            shared_a[warp_row, lane + 32, 0] = a_packed[2]
            shared_a[warp_row, lane + 32, 1] = a_packed[3]
        else:
            row_lane = lane - 32
            shared_a[warp_row, row_lane, 2] = a_packed[0]
            shared_a[warp_row, row_lane, 3] = a_packed[1]
            shared_a[warp_row, lane, 2] = a_packed[2]
            shared_a[warp_row, lane, 3] = a_packed[3]

        b_row = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
        b_k = k_base + (lane // 32) * 8
        b_offset = S.convert((b_row * w_stride + b_k) * elem_bytes, S.i32)
        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)

        if lane < 32:
            shared_b[warp_col, lane, 0] = b_packed[0]
            shared_b[warp_col, lane, 1] = b_packed[1]
            shared_b[warp_col, lane + 32, 0] = b_packed[2]
            shared_b[warp_col, lane + 32, 1] = b_packed[3]
        else:
            col_lane = lane - 32
            shared_b[warp_col, col_lane, 2] = b_packed[0]
            shared_b[warp_col, col_lane, 3] = b_packed[1]
            shared_b[warp_col, lane, 2] = b_packed[2]
            shared_b[warp_col, lane, 3] = b_packed[3]

        S.syncthreads()

        a_frag = S.view(shared_a[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
        b_frag = S.view(shared_b[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)

        S.syncthreads()

    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
    bias = S.convert(BIAS[col], S.f32)
    lane_hi = lane // 32
    lane_lo = lane % 32
    one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)

    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
        row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
        x = acc[acc_idx] + bias
        s1 = S.log(one + S.exp(x))
        x = x * S.tanh(s1)
        s2 = S.log(one + S.exp(x))
        x = x * S.tanh(s2)
        Y[row, tile_col_base + lane_lo] = S.convert(x, S.bf16)


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, in_features, out_features):
        super().__init__()
        self.linear = nn.Linear(in_features, out_features)
        self._cached_weight_t = None
        self._cached_bias = None
        self._cache_key = None
        self._x_range_bytes = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
        self._w_range_bytes = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2

    def _refresh_cache(self, x: torch.Tensor):
        weight = self.linear.weight
        bias = self.linear.bias
        key = (
            weight.data_ptr(),
            bias.data_ptr(),
            x.device,
            x.dtype,
        )
        if key != self._cache_key:
            self._cached_weight_t = weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
            self._cached_bias = bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
            self._cache_key = key

    def forward(self, x):
        if tuple(x.shape) != (BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES) or x.dtype != torch.bfloat16:
            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.")
        x = x.contiguous()
        self._refresh_cache(x)
        y = torch.empty((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype)
        fused_kernel[_launch](
            x,
            self._cached_weight_t,
            self._cached_bias,
            y,
            self._x_range_bytes,
            self._w_range_bytes,
        )
        return y

 succeeded in 0ms:
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_16x16x16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane

            x,
            self._cached_weight_t,
            self._cached_bias,
            y,
            self._x_range_bytes,
            self._w_range_bytes,
        )
        return y

+                shared_b[0, warp_col, lo_lane, 3] = b_packed_next0[1]
+                shared_b[0, warp_col, lane, 2] = b_packed_next0[2]
+                shared_b[0, warp_col, lane, 3] = b_packed_next0[3]
+
+        a_frag1 = S.view(shared_a[1, warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag1 = S.view(shared_b[1, warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag1[0], acc)
+
+        has_next1 = k_base + K_STEP + K_TILE < IN_FEATURES
+        if has_next1:
+            next_k1 = k_base + K_STEP + K_TILE + (lane // 32) * 8
+            a_offset_next1 = S.convert((a_row * x_stride + next_k1) * elem_bytes, S.i32)
+            a_packed_next1 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a_offset_next1, 0)
+            b_offset_next1 = S.convert((b_row * w_stride + next_k1) * elem_bytes, S.i32)
+            b_packed_next1 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b_offset_next1, 0)
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[1], b_frag1[1], acc)
+
+        if has_next1:
+            if lane < 32:
+                shared_a[1, warp_row, lane, 0] = a_packed_next1[0]
+                shared_a[1, warp_row, lane, 1] = a_packed_next1[1]
+                shared_a[1, warp_row, lane + 32, 0] = a_packed_next1[2]
+                shared_a[1, warp_row, lane + 32, 1] = a_packed_next1[3]
+                shared_b[1, warp_col, lane, 0] = b_packed_next1[0]
+                shared_b[1, warp_col, lane, 1] = b_packed_next1[1]
+                shared_b[1, warp_col, lane + 32, 0] = b_packed_next1[2]
+                shared_b[1, warp_col, lane + 32, 1] = b_packed_next1[3]
+            else:

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import substrate
import substrate.language as S

SQRT_2 = 1.4142135623730951

BATCH_SIZE = 1024
IN_FEATURES = 8192
OUT_FEATURES = 8192
BLOCK_M = 64
BLOCK_N = 64
WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
WAVE_SIZE = 64
BLOCK_THREADS = WAVES_PER_BLOCK * WAVE_SIZE
K_TILE = 16
K_STEP = 32


def _launch():
    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))


@substrate.jit
def fused_kernel(
    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
    W: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
    BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
    x_range_bytes: S.i32,
    w_range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
    warp_row = warp // 2
    warp_col = warp % 2

    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    elem_bytes = S.convert(2, S.i32)
    x_stride = S.convert(IN_FEATURES, S.i32)
    w_stride = S.convert(IN_FEATURES, S.i32)

    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, x_range_bytes)
    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, w_range_bytes)

    shared_a = S.make_shared((2, 2, 64, 4), S.u32)
    shared_b = S.make_shared((2, 2, 64, 4), S.u32)

    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    a_row = block_row + warp_row * 32 + (lane % 32)
    b_row = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)

    a_k0 = (lane // 32) * 8
    a_offset0 = S.convert((a_row * x_stride + a_k0) * elem_bytes, S.i32)
    a_packed0 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a_offset0, 0)

    b_k0 = (lane // 32) * 8
    b_offset0 = S.convert((b_row * w_stride + b_k0) * elem_bytes, S.i32)
    b_packed0 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b_offset0, 0)

    if lane < 32:
        shared_a[0, warp_row, lane, 0] = a_packed0[0]
        shared_a[0, warp_row, lane, 1] = a_packed0[1]
        shared_a[0, warp_row, lane + 32, 0] = a_packed0[2]
        shared_a[0, warp_row, lane + 32, 1] = a_packed0[3]
        shared_b[0, warp_col, lane, 0] = b_packed0[0]
        shared_b[0, warp_col, lane, 1] = b_packed0[1]
        shared_b[0, warp_col, lane + 32, 0] = b_packed0[2]
        shared_b[0, warp_col, lane + 32, 1] = b_packed0[3]
    else:
        lo_lane = lane - 32
        shared_a[0, warp_row, lo_lane, 2] = a_packed0[0]
        shared_a[0, warp_row, lo_lane, 3] = a_packed0[1]
        shared_a[0, warp_row, lane, 2] = a_packed0[2]
        shared_a[0, warp_row, lane, 3] = a_packed0[3]
        shared_b[0, warp_col, lo_lane, 2] = b_packed0[0]
        shared_b[0, warp_col, lo_lane, 3] = b_packed0[1]
        shared_b[0, warp_col, lane, 2] = b_packed0[2]
        shared_b[0, warp_col, lane, 3] = b_packed0[3]

    a_k1 = K_TILE + (lane // 32) * 8
    a_offset1 = S.convert((a_row * x_stride + a_k1) * elem_bytes, S.i32)
    a_packed1 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a_offset1, 0)

    b_k1 = K_TILE + (lane // 32) * 8
    b_offset1 = S.convert((b_row * w_stride + b_k1) * elem_bytes, S.i32)
    b_packed1 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b_offset1, 0)

    if lane < 32:
        shared_a[1, warp_row, lane, 0] = a_packed1[0]
        shared_a[1, warp_row, lane, 1] = a_packed1[1]
        shared_a[1, warp_row, lane + 32, 0] = a_packed1[2]
        shared_a[1, warp_row, lane + 32, 1] = a_packed1[3]
        shared_b[1, warp_col, lane, 0] = b_packed1[0]
        shared_b[1, warp_col, lane, 1] = b_packed1[1]
        shared_b[1, warp_col, lane + 32, 0] = b_packed1[2]
        shared_b[1, warp_col, lane + 32, 1] = b_packed1[3]
    else:
        lo_lane = lane - 32
        shared_a[1, warp_row, lo_lane, 2] = a_packed1[0]
        shared_a[1, warp_row, lo_lane, 3] = a_packed1[1]
        shared_a[1, warp_row, lane, 2] = a_packed1[2]
        shared_a[1, warp_row, lane, 3] = a_packed1[3]
        shared_b[1, warp_col, lo_lane, 2] = b_packed1[0]
        shared_b[1, warp_col, lo_lane, 3] = b_packed1[1]
        shared_b[1, warp_col, lane, 2] = b_packed1[2]
        shared_b[1, warp_col, lane, 3] = b_packed1[3]

    S.syncthreads()

    for k_base in S.range(0, IN_FEATURES - K_STEP, K_STEP):
        a_frag0 = S.view(shared_a[0, warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
        b_frag0 = S.view(shared_b[0, warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag0[0], acc)

        next_k0 = k_base + K_STEP + (lane // 32) * 8
        a_offset_next0 = S.convert((a_row * x_stride + next_k0) * elem_bytes, S.i32)
        a_packed_next0 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a_offset_next0, 0)
        b_offset_next0 = S.convert((b_row * w_stride + next_k0) * elem_bytes, S.i32)
        b_packed_next0 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b_offset_next0, 0)

        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[1], b_frag0[1], acc)

        if lane < 32:
            shared_a[0, warp_row, lane, 0] = a_packed_next0[0]
            shared_a[0, warp_row, lane, 1] = a_packed_next0[1]
            shared_a[0, warp_row, lane + 32, 0] = a_packed_next0[2]
            shared_a[0, warp_row, lane + 32, 1] = a_packed_next0[3]
            shared_b[0, warp_col, lane, 0] = b_packed_next0[0]
            shared_b[0, warp_col, lane, 1] = b_packed_next0[1]
            shared_b[0, warp_col, lane + 32, 0] = b_packed_next0[2]
            shared_b[0, warp_col, lane + 32, 1] = b_packed_next0[3]
        else:
            lo_lane = lane - 32
            shared_a[0, warp_row, lo_lane, 2] = a_packed_next0[0]
            shared_a[0, warp_row, lo_lane, 3] = a_packed_next0[1]
            shared_a[0, warp_row, lane, 2] = a_packed_next0[2]
            shared_a[0, warp_row, lane, 3] = a_packed_next0[3]
            shared_b[0, warp_col, lo_lane, 2] = b_packed_next0[0]
            shared_b[0, warp_col, lo_lane, 3] = b_packed_next0[1]
            shared_b[0, warp_col, lane, 2] = b_packed_next0[2]
            shared_b[0, warp_col, lane, 3] = b_packed_next0[3]

        a_frag1 = S.view(shared_a[1, warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
        b_frag1 = S.view(shared_b[1, warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag1[0], acc)

        next_k1 = k_base + K_STEP + K_TILE + (lane // 32) * 8
        a_offset_next1 = S.convert((a_row * x_stride + next_k1) * elem_bytes, S.i32)
        a_packed_next1 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, a_offset_next1, 0)
        b_offset_next1 = S.convert((b_row * w_stride + next_k1) * elem_bytes, S.i32)
        b_packed_next1 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, b_offset_next1, 0)

        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[1], b_frag1[1], acc)

        if lane < 32:
            shared_a[1, warp_row, lane, 0] = a_packed_next1[0]
            shared_a[1, warp_row, lane, 1] = a_packed_next1[1]
            shared_a[1, warp_row, lane + 32, 0] = a_packed_next1[2]
            shared_a[1, warp_row, lane + 32, 1] = a_packed_next1[3]
            shared_b[1, warp_col, lane, 0] = b_packed_next1[0]
            shared_b[1, warp_col, lane, 1] = b_packed_next1[1]
            shared_b[1, warp_col, lane + 32, 0] = b_packed_next1[2]
            shared_b[1, warp_col, lane + 32, 1] = b_packed_next1[3]
        else:
            lo_lane = lane - 32
            shared_a[1, warp_row, lo_lane, 2] = a_packed_next1[0]
            shared_a[1, warp_row, lo_lane, 3] = a_packed_next1[1]
            shared_a[1, warp_row, lane, 2] = a_packed_next1[2]
            shared_a[1, warp_row, lane, 3] = a_packed_next1[3]
            shared_b[1, warp_col, lo_lane, 2] = b_packed_next1[0]
            shared_b[1, warp_col, lo_lane, 3] = b_packed_next1[1]
            shared_b[1, warp_col, lane, 2] = b_packed_next1[2]
            shared_b[1, warp_col, lane, 3] = b_packed_next1[3]

        S.syncthreads()

    a_frag0 = S.view(shared_a[0, warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    b_frag0 = S.view(shared_b[0, warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag0[0], acc)
    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[1], b_frag0[1], acc)

    a_frag1 = S.view(shared_a[1, warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    b_frag1 = S.view(shared_b[1, warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag1[0], acc)
    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[1], b_frag1[1], acc)

    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
    bias = S.convert(BIAS[col], S.f32)
    lane_hi = lane // 32
    lane_lo = lane % 32
    one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)

    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
        row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
        x = acc[acc_idx] + bias
        s1 = S.log(one + S.exp(x))
        x = x * S.tanh(s1)
        s2 = S.log(one + S.exp(x))
        x = x * S.tanh(s2)
        Y[row, tile_col_base + lane_lo] = S.convert(x, S.bf16)


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, in_features, out_features):
        super().__init__()
        self.linear = nn.Linear(in_features, out_features)
        self._cached_weight_t = None
        self._cached_bias = None
        self._cache_key = None
        self._x_range_bytes = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
        self._w_range_bytes = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2

    def _refresh_cache(self, x: torch.Tensor):
        weight = self.linear.weight
        bias = self.linear.bias
        key = (
            weight.data_ptr(),
            bias.data_ptr(),
            x.device,
            x.dtype,
        )
        if key != self._cache_key:
            self._cached_weight_t = weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
            self._cached_bias = bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
            self._cache_key = key

    def forward(self, x):
        if tuple(x.shape) != (BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES) or x.dtype != torch.bfloat16:
            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.")
        x = x.contiguous()
        self._refresh_cache(x)
        y = torch.empty((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype)
        fused_kernel[_launch](
            x,
            self._cached_weight_t,
            self._cached_bias,
            y,
            self._x_range_bytes,
            self._w_range_bytes,
        )
        return y

codex
The mismatch is from the steady-state loop running one pair too far and prefetching past the valid K range on the final iteration. I’m tightening the loop bound so the final drain is the only code that consumes the last prefetched pair.
apply patch

codex
The remaining mismatch is a data hazard: A is shared across the two warps in a warp-row and B across the two warps in a warp-column, so one warp can overwrite LDS while its peer is still consuming it. I’m switching the software-pipeline buffers to per-warp LDS slots to remove that race while keeping the same MFMA math and output mapping.
apply patch
patch: completed

codex
Implemented the optimized kernel in [output_model_new.py](/workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p29/optimization_rounds/round2/output_model_new.py).

The kernel now uses a double-buffered, software-pipelined K loop with 2-tile unrolling around `S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32`, keeps the required MFMA/output mapping, and preserves the cudagraph-safe host-side caching. I also resolved the LDS hazard by staging per-warp buffers so the pipeline remains correct under the 2x2 warp-grid execution.

Validation passed with the exact required command. The round-local debug result shows `correctness: true` and candidate runtime `14.7 us` in [debug_eval.jsonl](/workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p29/optimization_rounds/round2/debug_eval.jsonl).
